ConfigDef Annotation Pattern in Apache Kafka\\n\\nApache Kafka uses a comprehensive configuration system based on the ConfigDef and ConfigKey classes (located in clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/) rather than traditional Java annotations. This pattern defines configuration metadata including names, types, defaults, validators, documentation, and importance levels.\\n\\n### Core Infrastructure\\n\\n**1. ConfigDef.java** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/ConfigDef.java)\\n- Main configuration definition class that manages a collection of ConfigKey objects\\n- Contains the ConfigKey inner class (public static class ConfigKey) which represents individual configuration entries\\n- Provides documentation generation methods: toHtml(), toHtmlTable(), and related methods for generating HTML documentation from configuration metadata\\n- Supports validation through Validator interface and recommendations through Recommender interface\\n- ConfigKey properties: name, type, defaultValue, validator, importance, documentation, group, orderInGroup, width, displayName, dependents, recommender, internalConfig\\n\\n**2. AbstractConfig.java** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/AbstractConfig.java)\\n- Base class for all configuration implementations\\n- Holds original configuration values and parsed/validated values\\n- Provides methods for accessing config values: getString(), getInt(), getBoolean(), etc.\\n- Integrates with ConfigDef for validation and type conversion\\n- Supports config provider resolution for dynamic value substitution\\n\\n### Configuration Pattern\\n\\nEach configuration class follows a consistent pattern:\\n1. Defines a static ConfigDef field (CONFIG, CONFIG_DEF, or similar)\\n2. Uses ConfigDef.define() to add individual configuration keys with metadata\\n3. Either extends AbstractConfig directly or extends a specialized config base class\\n4. Provides a public static configDef() method to return the ConfigDef instance\\n\\n### Major Config Classes (46 total found)\\n\\n**Clients Module:**\\n- AdminClientConfig - Client admin operations configuration\\n- ConsumerConfig - Consumer client configuration\\n- ProducerConfig - Producer client configuration\\n- BrokerSecurityConfigs - Security-related configurations\\n\\n**Server Module:**\\n- AbstractKafkaConfig - Base configuration for Kafka servers\\n- KRaftConfigs - KRaft mode configurations\\n- ServerConfigs - Core server configurations\\n- SocketServerConfigs - Network/socket configurations\\n- ClientMetricsConfigs - Client metrics tracking\\n- MetricConfigs - JMX and metrics configurations\\n- DelegationTokenManagerConfigs - Token management\\n- ReplicationConfigs - Replication parameters\\n\\n**Streams Module:**\\n- StreamsConfig - Kafka Streams application configuration\\n- TopologyConfig - Topology-specific settings\\n\\n**Connect Module:**\\n- WorkerConfig - Kafka Connect worker configuration (base)\\n- ConnectorConfig - Base connector configuration\\n- SourceConnectorConfig - Source-specific configuration\\n- SinkConnectorConfig - Sink-specific configuration\\n- TaskConfig - Task configuration\\n- RestServerConfig - REST endpoint configuration\\n- StandaloneConfig - Standalone worker configuration\\n- DistributedConfig - Distributed worker configuration\\n- SimpleConfig - Simplified configuration wrapper\\n- MirrorClientConfig, MirrorConnectorConfig, MirrorMakerConfig - Mirror Maker configurations\\n\\n**Coordinator Modules:**\\n- GroupCoordinatorConfig - Consumer group coordination\\n- GroupConfig - Group-level settings\\n- ShareGroupConfig - Share group settings\\n- ShareCoordinatorConfig - Share group coordination\\n- TransactionLogConfig, TransactionStateManagerConfig, AddPartitionsToTxnConfig - Transaction management\\n\\n**Storage/Log Module:**\\n- LogConfig - Topic log configuration\\n- CleanerConfig - Log cleaner configuration\\n- RemoteLogManagerConfig - Remote log tier storage\\n\\n**Raft Module:**\\n- QuorumConfig - Raft quorum configuration\\n- MetadataLogConfig - Metadata log configuration\\n\\n### Documentation Generation Chain\\n\\nThe documentation generation system works through:\\n1. ConfigDef.toHtml() method converts config metadata to HTML\\n2. Used by KafkaConfig.main() to generate broker config docs\\n3. Used by StreamsConfig.main() to generate streams config docs\\n4. Used by ConsumerConfig, ProducerConfig, LogConfig main methods\\n5. Used by ConnectorConfig documentation system\\n\\nThis pattern allows centralized, consistent configuration documentation generation from the same metadata source.\"\n   219→}\n   220→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware.
